# <a name="exchange-online-service-description"></a><span data-ttu-id="1f23f-105">Descrição de serviço do Exchange Online</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-105">Exchange Online service description</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-106">Você está procurando uma comparação de recursos de assinaturas que incluam o Exchange Online?</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-106">Are you looking for a feature comparison of subscriptions that include Exchange Online?</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1f23f-107">Nesse caso, o artigo de descrição do serviço Exchange Online é o que você procura.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-107">If so, the Exchange Online service description article is what you need.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1f23f-108">Você também aprenderá sobre requisitos do sistema, bem como requisitos de armazenamento e de destinatário.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-108">You'll also learn about system requirements as well as storage and recipient requirements.</span></span>
  
> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="1f23f-109">Se você precisar de ajuda com uma tarefa ou se estiver solucionando um problema, poderá encontrar os seguintes recursos úteis:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-109">If you need assistance with a task, or if you are troubleshooting a problem, you might find the following resources helpful:</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-110">[Email](https://support.office.com/article/Email-94275804-7147-4332-9ccd-5d421760a9ed) para ajudar a criar e enviar emails.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-110">[Email](https://support.office.com/article/Email-94275804-7147-4332-9ccd-5d421760a9ed) for help creating and sending email.</span></span> <br/><span data-ttu-id="1f23f-111"> 
[Gerenciar emails e calendários](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/admin/email/email)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-111">

[Sobre o Assistente de Recuperação e Suporte da Microsoft](https://diagnostics.office.com/)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-112"> 
[About the Microsoft Support and Recovery Assistant](https://diagnostics.office.com/)</span></span><br/><span data-ttu-id="1f23f-113"> 
[Relatórios de não entrega de email no Exchange Online](https://docs.microsoft.com/Exchange/mail-flow-best-practices/non-delivery-reports-in-exchange-online/non-delivery-reports-in-exchange-online)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-113"> 
[Email non-delivery reports in Exchange Online](https://docs.microsoft.com/Exchange/mail-flow-best-practices/non-delivery-reports-in-exchange-online/non-delivery-reports-in-exchange-online)</span></span><br/><span data-ttu-id="1f23f-114"> 
[Ajuda do Exchange Online](https://docs.microsoft.com/exchange/exchange-online)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-114"> 
[Exchange Online Help](https://docs.microsoft.com/exchange/exchange-online)</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-p104">Microsoft Exchange Online é uma solução de mensagens hospedada que fornece o recursos do Microsoft Exchange Server como um serviço baseado em nuvem. Isso permite que os usuários acessem o e-mail, o calendário, os contatos e as tarefas a partir de computadores, da Web e de dispositivos móveis. Ele se integra totalmente ao Active Directory, permitindo que os administradores usem políticas de grupo, bem como outras ferramentas administrativas, para gerenciar os recursos do Exchange Online em seu ambiente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-p104">Microsoft Exchange Online is a hosted messaging solution that delivers the capabilities of Microsoft Exchange Server as a cloud-based service. It gives users access to email, calendar, contacts, and tasks from PCs, the web, and mobile devices. It integrates fully with Active Directory, enabling administrators to use group policies, as well as other administration tools, to manage Exchange Online features across their environment.</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-118">As organizações que assinam o Exchange Online mantêm controle sobre os serviços de mensagens que oferecem aos usuários, mas elas não têm a carga operacional de software de servidor local.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-118">Organizations that subscribe to Exchange Online retain control over the messaging services they offer to users, but they do not have the operational burden of on-premises server software.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1f23f-119">Com os planos hospedados do Exchange Online descritos neste documento, o email é hospedado em servidores que dão suporte a vários clientes simultaneamente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-119">With the Exchange Online hosted plans described in this document, email is hosted on servers that support multiple customers simultaneously.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1f23f-120">Esses servidores são ativos nos data centers da Microsoft e são acessíveis aos usuários em uma ampla variedade de dispositivos de dentro de uma rede corporativa ou pela Internet.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-120">These servers are housed in Microsoft data centers and are accessible to users on a wide range of devices from inside a corporate network or over the internet.</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-121">Para comparar recursos entre planos, consulte [Ferramentas poderosas para dar suporte à sua empresa.](https://products.office.com/business/compare-more-office-365-for-business-plans)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-121">To compare features across plans, see [Powerful tools to support your enterprise](https://products.office.com/business/compare-more-office-365-for-business-plans).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1f23f-122">Para comparar os planos do Office 365 Germany, confira [Planos de assinatura do Office 365 Germany](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=839016).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-122">To compare plans for Office 365 Germany, see [Office 365 Germany subscription plans](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=839016).</span></span>
  
> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="1f23f-123">Você pode exportar, salvar e imprimir páginas nas descrições de serviço da Microsoft.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-123">You can export, save, and print pages in the Microsoft service descriptions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1f23f-124">Saiba como exportar [resultados da Pesquisa de Conteúdo.](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/securitycompliance/export-search-results)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-124">Learn how to [Export Content Search results](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/securitycompliance/export-search-results).</span></span> 
  
## <a name="whats-new-in-exchange-admin-center"></a><span data-ttu-id="1f23f-125">Novidades do centro de administração do Exchange</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-125">What's new in Exchange admin center</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-126">Para obter informações sobre novos recursos no Centro de administração do Exchange, consulte [Novidades no Centro de administração do Exchange](https://docs.microsoft.com/exchange/whats-new).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-126">For information about new features in Exchange admin center, see [What's new in Exchange admin center](https://docs.microsoft.com/exchange/whats-new).</span></span>
  
## <a name="plans-for-exchange-online"></a><span data-ttu-id="1f23f-127">Planos para o Exchange Online</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-127">Plans for Exchange Online</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-128">O Microsoft 365 está disponível em uma variedade de planos para atender melhor às necessidades da sua organização.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-128">Microsoft 365 is available in a variety of plans to best meet the needs of your organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1f23f-129">Para obter informações detalhadas sobre o plano sobre assinaturas que habilitam usuários para o Exchange Online, consulte a tabela de comparação [de assinatura completa](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=2139145).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-129">For detailed plan information on subscriptions that enable users for Exchange Online, see the [full subscription comparison table](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=2139145).</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-p109">Cada usuário que acessar o serviço Exchange Online deve ser atribuído a um plano de assinatura, e cada assinatura de usuário ter sua própria caixa de correio. Pastas e mensagens nessas caixas de correio residem em um computador com Exchange Server em um data center da Microsoft.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-p109">Each user who accesses the Exchange Online service must be assigned to a subscription plan, and each user subscription has its own mailbox. Folders and messages in these mailboxes reside on a computer running Exchange Server at a Microsoft data center.</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-p110">As assinaturas do usuário não são exigidas para salas de conferência e caixas de correio compartilhadas. Esses tipos de caixa de correio especial não têm credenciais de logon. Em vez disso, os usuários licenciados com as permissões apropriadas gerenciam e acessam essas caixas por meio de delegação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-p110">User subscriptions are not required for conference rooms and shared mailboxes. These special mailbox types do not have login credentials. Instead, licensed users with the appropriate permissions manage and access them via delegation.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-135">**Direitos de uso da caixa de correio de usuário do Microsoft 365 F1**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-135">**Microsoft 365 F1 User Mailbox Use Rights**</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-136">O Microsoft 365 F1 não inclui direitos para uma caixa de correio do Exchange.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-136">Microsoft 365 F1 does not include rights to an Exchange mailbox.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1f23f-137">Para habilitar uma experiência completa do Teams, as licenças do M365 F1 podem vir com o plano de serviço K1 do Exchange Online habilitado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-137">In order to enable a full Teams experience, M365 F1 licenses may come with the Exchange Online K1 service plan enabled.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1f23f-138">Embora o plano de serviço K1 do Exchange Online provisione uma caixa de correio para o usuário, os usuários do M365 F1 não têm o direito de usar a caixa de correio.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-138">Although the Exchange Online K1 service plan will provision a mailbox for the user, M365 F1 users are not entitled to use the mailbox.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1f23f-139">Recomendamos que você desabilite o Outlook na Web [por](https://docs.microsoft.com/exchange/recipients-in-exchange-online/manage-user-mailboxes/enable-or-disable-outlook-web-app) meio dessas etapas e peça aos usuários que não acessem a caixa de correio do Exchange por meio de outros métodos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-139">We recommend that you disable Outlook on the web via [these steps](https://docs.microsoft.com/exchange/recipients-in-exchange-online/manage-user-mailboxes/enable-or-disable-outlook-web-app) and ask your users not to access the Exchange mailbox via any other methods.</span></span>
  
## <a name="system-requirements-for-exchange-online"></a><span data-ttu-id="1f23f-140">Requisitos do sistema do Exchange Online</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-140">System requirements for Exchange Online</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-141">Para requisitos do sistema, o serviço mensal baseado em assinatura disponível para empresas, educação e organizações governamentais, consulte [Microsoft 365 and Office Resources](https://products.office.com/office-system-requirements/#Office365forBEG).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-141">For system requirements, the monthly subscription-based service available for business, education, and government organizations, please see [Microsoft 365 and Office Resources](https://products.office.com/office-system-requirements/#Office365forBEG).</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1085">Complementos do Outlook e MAPI do Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1085">Outlook add-ins and Outlook MAPI</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1086">Sim<sup>19</sup></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1086">Yes<sup>19</sup></span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1087">Sim</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1087">Yes</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1088">Sim<sup>19</sup></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1088">Yes<sup>19</sup></span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1089">Sim<sup>19</sup></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1089">Yes<sup>19</sup></span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1090">Sim<sup>19</sup></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1090">Yes<sup>19</sup></span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1091">Sim<sup>19</sup></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1091">Yes<sup>19</sup></span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1092">Sim<sup>19</sup></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1092">Yes<sup>19</sup></span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1093">Não</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1093">No</span></span>|

<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1094"><sup>1</sup> Requer uma assinatura Arquivamento do Exchange Online para cada usuário de caixa de correio local que tenha um arquivo morto baseado em nuvem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1094"><sup>1</sup> Requires an Exchange Online Archiving subscription for each on-premises mailbox user that has a cloud-based archive.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1095"><sup>2</sup> A Proteção de Informações do Azure não está incluída, mas pode ser comprada como um complemento separado e permitirá os recursos de Gerenciamento de Direitos de Informação (IRM) com suporte.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1095"><sup>2</sup> Azure Information Protection is not included, but it can be purchased as a separate add-on and will enable the supported Information Rights Management (IRM) features.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1096">Alguns recursos da Proteção de Informações do Azure exigem uma assinatura do Microsoft 365 Apps para empresas, que não está incluída no Microsoft 365 Business Basic, no Microsoft 365 Business Standard, no Office 365 Enterprise E1, no Office 365 Education ou no Office 365 Enterprise F3.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1096">Some Azure Information Protection features require a subscription to Microsoft 365 Apps for enterprise, which is not included with Microsoft 365 Business Basic, Microsoft 365 Business Standard, Office 365 Enterprise E1, Office 365 Education, or Office 365 Enterprise F3.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1097"><sup>3</sup> O Windows Server AD RMS é um servidor local que precisa ser adquirido e gerenciado separadamente de forma a permitir os recursos de IRM com suporte.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1097"><sup>3</sup> Windows Server AD RMS is an on-premises server that must be purchased and managed separately in order to enable the supported IRM features.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1098"><sup>4</sup> As regras de transporte são feitas de critérios flexíveis, que permitem definir condições e exceções e ações a tomar com base nos critérios.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1098"><sup>4</sup> Transport rules are made up of flexible criteria, which allow you to define conditions and exceptions, and actions to take based on the criteria.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1099">Os critérios e ações disponíveis diferem entre o Exchange Online e Microsoft Exchange Server 2013.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1099">The available criteria and actions differ between Exchange Online, and Microsoft Exchange Server 2013.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1100">Para ver a lista de critérios e ações disponíveis, confira os tópicos correspondentes sobre critérios e ações para cada produto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1100">For a list of available criteria and actions, see the corresponding criteria and actions topics for each product.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1101"><sup>5</sup> Para o Exchange 2013, a DLP requer uma Licença de Acesso para Cliente do Exchange Enterprise (CAL).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1101"><sup>5</sup> For Exchange 2013, DLP requires an Exchange Enterprise Client Access License (CAL).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1102">Para obter mais informações sobre CALs e licenciamento de servidor, consulte [Perguntas frequentes sobre licenciamento do Exchange.](https://products.office.com/exchange/microsoft-exchange-licensing-faq-email-for-business)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1102">For more information about CALs and server licensing, see [Exchange licensing FAQs](https://products.office.com/exchange/microsoft-exchange-licensing-faq-email-for-business).</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1103"><sup>6</sup> Exchange Server 2013 tem a maioria dos mesmos recursos anti-spam integrados que Exchange Server 2010.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1103"><sup>6</sup> Exchange Server 2013 has most of the same built-in anti-spam capabilities as Exchange Server 2010.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1104">Para obter informações sobre os benefícios da filtragem de spam hospedada pelo Exchange sobre as ofertas locais, consulte Benefícios dos recursos [anti-spam no Exchange Online Protection Over Exchange Server 2013](https://docs.microsoft.com/exchange/benefits-of-anti-spam-features-in-exchange-online-protection-over-exchange-server-2013-exchange-2013-help).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1104">For information about the benefits of Exchange hosted spam filtering over the on-premises offerings, see [Benefits of Anti-Spam Features in Exchange Online Protection Over Exchange Server 2013](https://docs.microsoft.com/exchange/benefits-of-anti-spam-features-in-exchange-online-protection-over-exchange-server-2013-exchange-2013-help).</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1105"><sup>7</sup> Somente acessível por meio de acesso direto à interface de gerenciamento do Centro de administração do Exchange (EAC).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1105"><sup>7</sup> Only accessible via direct access to the Exchange admin center (EAC) management interface.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1106"><sup>8</sup> Exchange Server 2013 usa apenas o mecanismo anti-malware da Microsoft.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1106"><sup>8</sup> Exchange Server 2013 uses only the Microsoft anti-malware engine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1107">O Exchange Online usa diversos mecanismos antimalware para verificar se há malware em mensagens de entrada, saída e internas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1107">Exchange Online uses multiple anti-malware engines to scan inbound, outbound, and internal messages for malware.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1108"><sup>9</sup> Uma assinatura EOA pode ser comprada separadamente para cada caixa de correio que exige a caixa de correio inativa ou o recurso de arquivo morto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1108"><sup>9</sup> An EOA subscription can be purchased separately for each mailbox that requires either the inactive mailbox or archive feature.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1109"><sup>10</sup> O SharePoint deve ser implantado na organização local do Exchange.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1109"><sup>10</sup> SharePoint must be deployed in the on-premises Exchange organization.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1110"><sup>11</sup> O SharePoint Online deve ser incluído no plano de assinatura.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1110"><sup>11</sup> SharePoint Online must be included in the subscription plan.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1111"><sup>12</sup> POP é suportado, mas IMAP não é.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1111"><sup>12</sup> POP is supported, but IMAP is not.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1112"><sup>13</sup> Suportado para clientes Exchange Server 2013 locais que compram a Proteção de Informações do Azure.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1112"><sup>13</sup> Supported for Exchange Server 2013 on-premises customers who purchase Azure Information Protection.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1113">A Criptografia de Mensagens do Office 365 exige que os clientes locais roteem emails por meio do Exchange Online, usando a Proteção do Exchange Online para filtragem de email ou estabelecendo o fluxo de emails híbrido.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1113">Office 365 Message Encryption requires on-premises customers to route email through Exchange Online, either by using Exchange Online Protection for email filtering, or by establishing hybrid mail flow.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1114"><sup>14</sup> Exchange Server 2013 os clientes precisam baixar e instalar o SP1 para acessar a Impressão Digital de Documento e Dicas de Política no OWA e no OWA para Dispositivos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1114"><sup>14</sup> Exchange Server 2013 customers need to download and install SP1 in order to access Document Fingerprinting and Policy Tips in OWA and OWA for Devices.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1115"><sup>15</sup> BitLocker Drive Encryption é suportado para Exchange Server 2013, mas um administrador precisa habilitar o recurso.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1115"><sup>15</sup> BitLocker Drive Encryption is supported for Exchange Server 2013, but an administrator needs to enable the feature.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1116"><sup>16</sup> O Microsoft 365 Business Basic, o Microsoft 365 Business Standard e o Office 365 Enterprise F3 não fornecem direitos de acesso para utilização com servidores locais.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1116"><sup>16</sup> Microsoft 365 Business Basic, Microsoft 365 Business Standard, and Office 365 Enterprise F3 do not provide access rights for utilization with on-premises servers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1117">Para estar em conformidade, o cliente deve comprar ou ter comprado previamente as CALs apropriadas ou atualizar para um SKU Enterprise, que fornece esses direitos de acesso.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1117">To be compliant, customer must purchase or have previously purchased the appropriate CALs or upgrade to an Enterprise SKU that provides these access rights.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1118"><sup>17</sup> Contas conectadas são suportadas para contas &amp; IMAP POP, mas desabilitadas para Outlook.com (Hotmail).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1118"><sup>17</sup> Connected accounts are supported for POP &amp; IMAP accounts, but disabled for Outlook.com (Hotmail).</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1119"><sup>18</sup> Não há suporte para usar cmdlets no PowerShell do Exchange Online para personalizar as listas de endereços padrão e a GAL (lista de endereços global) padrão.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1119"><sup>18</sup> Using cmdlets in Exchange Online PowerShell to customize the default address lists and the default global address list (GAL) is not supported.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1120"><sup>19</sup> Algumas Web Parts e complementos de terceiros podem não estar disponíveis.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1120"><sup>19</sup> Some third-party web parts and add-ins may not be available.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1121"><sup>20</sup> Para a Descoberta EDiscovery, você precisa de uma consulta separada para nuvem local versus local.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1121"><sup>20</sup> For eDiscovery, you need a separate query for on-premises vs. cloud.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1122"><sup>21</sup> A tabela indica se o cliente trabalha ou não com os planos associados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1122"><sup>21</sup> The table indicates whether or not the client works with the associated plans.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1123">Isso não significa que os clientes estejam necessariamente incluídos na compra desses planos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1123">It does not mean the clients are necessarily included in the purchase of these plans.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1124"><sup>22</sup> Para obter mais informações, consulte [Service encryption with Customer Key](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/securitycompliance/controlling-your-data-using-customer-key).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1124"><sup>22</sup> For more information, see [Service encryption with Customer Key](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/securitycompliance/controlling-your-data-using-customer-key).</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1125"><sup>23 O</sup> suporte à UM do Exchange Online para sistemas PBX de terceiros por meio de conexões diretas de SBCs operados pelo cliente terminará em abril de 2019.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1125"><sup>23</sup> Exchange Online UM support for third-party PBX systems via direct connections from customer operated SBCs will end in April 2019.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1126">Para obter mais informações, consulte o blog de equipe do Exchange [Descontinuação](https://techcommunity.microsoft.com/t5/Exchange-Team-Blog/New-date-for-discontinuation-of-support-for-Session-Border/ba-p/607853)do suporte para Controladores de Borda de Sessão na Unificação de Mensagens do Exchange Online.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1126">For more information, see the Exchange team blog [Discontinuation of support for Session Border Controllers in Exchange Online Unified Messaging](https://techcommunity.microsoft.com/t5/Exchange-Team-Blog/New-date-for-discontinuation-of-support-for-Session-Border/ba-p/607853).</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1127"><sup>24</sup> Um usuário F3 não pode adicionar representantes à sua própria caixa de correio, mas pode acessar outra caixa de correio (incluindo caixas de correio compartilhadas) e executar qualquer ação que tenha sido delegada a eles.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1127"><sup>24</sup> An F3 user cannot add delegates to their own mailbox, but they can access another mailbox (including shared mailboxes) and perform any actions that have been delegated to them.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1128"><sup>25</sup> Uma assinatura do Microsoft 365 Apps for enterprise também é necessária para o Exchange Server 2013 e Exchange Server 2016.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1128"><sup>25</sup> A subscription for Microsoft 365 Apps for enterprise is also required for Exchange Server 2013 and Exchange Server 2016.</span></span><br/>
<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1129"><sup>26 Suporte</sup> ao aplicativo EWS aplicado à representação de aplicativo EWS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1129"><sup>26</sup> EWS application support applied to EWS application impersonation.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1744"><sup>1</sup> As regras de transporte são feitas de critérios flexíveis, que permitem definir condições e exceções e ações a tomar com base nos critérios.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1744"><sup>1</sup> Transport rules are made up of flexible criteria, which allow you to define conditions and exceptions, and actions to take based on the criteria.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1745">Os critérios e ações disponíveis diferem entre o Exchange Online e Microsoft Exchange Server 2013.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1745">The available criteria and actions differ between Exchange Online, and Microsoft Exchange Server 2013.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1746">Para ver a lista de critérios e ações disponíveis, confira os tópicos correspondentes sobre critérios e ações para cada produto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1746">For a list of available criteria and actions, see the corresponding criteria and actions topics for each product.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1747"><sup>2</sup> Para obter informações sobre os benefícios da filtragem de spam hospedada pelo Exchange sobre as ofertas locais, consulte Benefícios dos recursos [anti-spam no Exchange Online Protection Over Exchange Server 2013](https://docs.microsoft.com/exchange/benefits-of-anti-spam-features-in-exchange-online-protection-over-exchange-server-2013-exchange-2013-help).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1747"><sup>2</sup> For information about the benefits of Exchange hosted spam filtering over the on-premises offerings, see [Benefits of Anti-Spam Features in Exchange Online Protection Over Exchange Server 2013](https://docs.microsoft.com/exchange/benefits-of-anti-spam-features-in-exchange-online-protection-over-exchange-server-2013-exchange-2013-help).</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1748"><sup>3</sup> O SharePoint deve ser implantado na organização local do Exchange.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1748"><sup>3</sup> SharePoint must be deployed in the on-premises Exchange organization.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1749"><sup>4</sup> O SharePoint Online deve ser incluído no plano de assinatura.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1749"><sup>4</sup> SharePoint Online must be included in the subscription plan.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1750"><sup>5</sup> Requer uma assinatura Arquivamento do Exchange Online para cada usuário de caixa de correio local que tenha um arquivo morto baseado em nuvem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1750"><sup>5</sup> Requires an Exchange Online Archiving subscription for each on-premises mailbox user that has a cloud-based archive.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1751"><sup>6</sup> Uma assinatura Arquivamento do Exchange Online pode ser comprada separadamente para cada caixa de correio que exige o recurso de caixa de correio inativa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1751"><sup>6</sup> An Exchange Online Archiving subscription can be purchased separately for each mailbox that requires the inactive mailbox feature.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1752"><sup>7</sup> Exchange Server 2013 usa apenas o mecanismo anti-malware da Microsoft.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1752"><sup>7</sup> Exchange Server 2013 uses only the Microsoft anti-malware engine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1753">O Exchange Online usa diversos mecanismos antimalware para verificar se há malware em mensagens de entrada, saída e internas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1753">Exchange Online uses multiple anti-malware engines to scan inbound, outbound, and internal messages for malware.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1754"><sup>8</sup> Somente acessível por meio de acesso direto à interface de gerenciamento do Centro de administração do Exchange (EAC).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1754"><sup>8</sup> Only accessible via direct access to the Exchange admin center (EAC) management interface.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1755">Não há suporte para IMAP <sup>9.</sup></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1755"><sup>9</sup> IMAP is not supported.</span></span> <br/>

<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1758"><sup>11</sup> A Proteção de Informações do Azure não está incluída, mas pode ser comprada como um complemento separado e permitirá os recursos de Gerenciamento de Direitos de Informação (IRM) com suporte.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1758"><sup>11</sup> Azure Information Protection is not included, but it can be purchased as a separate add-on and will enable the supported Information Rights Management (IRM) features.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1759">Alguns recursos da Proteção de Informações do Azure exigem uma assinatura do Microsoft 365 Apps para empresas, que não está incluída no Microsoft 365 Business Basic, no Microsoft 365 Business Standard, no Office 365 Enterprise E1, no Office 365 Education ou no Office 365 Enterprise F3.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1759">Some Azure Information Protection features require a subscription to Microsoft 365 Apps for enterprise, which is not included with Microsoft 365 Business Basic, Microsoft 365 Business Standard, Office 365 Enterprise E1, Office 365 Education, or Office 365 Enterprise F3.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1760">A Criptografia de Mensagens do Office 365 depende da Proteção de Informações do Azure.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1760">Office 365 Message Encryption depends on Azure Information Protection.</span></span> <br/>

<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1762"><sup>13</sup> Suportado para clientes que executam o Exchange Server 2013 ou posterior que compram a Proteção de Informações do Azure.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1762"><sup>13</sup> Supported for customers running Exchange Server 2013 or later who purchase Azure Information Protection.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1763">A Criptografia de Mensagens do Office 365 exige que os clientes locais roteem emails por meio do Exchange Online, usando a Proteção do Exchange Online para filtragem de email ou estabelecendo o fluxo de emails híbrido.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1763">Office 365 Message Encryption requires on-premises customers to route email through Exchange Online, either by using Exchange Online Protection for email filtering, or by establishing hybrid mail flow.</span></span> <br/>

<span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1774"><sup>23</sup> Quiosque do Exchange Online não fornece direitos de acesso para utilização com servidores locais.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1774"><sup>23</sup> Exchange Online Kiosk does not provide access rights for utilization with on-premises servers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1f23f-1775">Para estar em conformidade, o cliente deve comprar ou ter comprado previamente as CALs apropriadas ou atualizar para um SKU Enterprise, que fornece esses direitos de acesso.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1f23f-1775">To be compliant, customer must purchase or have previously purchased the appropriate CALs or upgrade to an Enterprise SKU that provides these access rights.</span></span> <br/>
